                console.debug('Classificacao: Feed Ready');
                classificacaoFeedReady = true;
                initCardClassificacao();
            });

            $(document).on('card-classificacao-ready', function() {
                console.debug('Classificacao: Card Ready');
                classificacaoCardReady = true;
                initCardClassificacao();
            });

        var initCardClassificacao = function(){
            if(classificacaoCardReady && classificacaoFeedReady){
                $('#ge-card-classificacao-8fc0a7f1-8e93-4d85-9d18-4e7e47d35123').show();
            }
        }
    }

    try {

      var classificacao = new CardClassificacao({
        context: '#ge-card-classificacao-8fc0a7f1-8e93-4d85-9d18-4e7e47d35123'
      });

      var classificacaoTracking = new CardClassificacaoTracking("8fc0a7f1-8e93-4d85-9d18-4e7e47d35123");

    } catch (err) {}

});
</script></div><div class="areatemplate-esquerda

    var glb_realtime_map = {
        site: 'globoesporte',
        categories: ['home'],
        url: 'http://globoesporte.globo.com/pe/futebol/times/sport/'
    };

    var realtime = function(realtimeLoaded, msg){
        if(realtimeLoaded){
            return;
        }

        $.getScript('http://s.glbimg.com/bu/rt/js/glb-rt.js', function(){
            $.ajax({
                dataType: 'jsonp',
                
                url: 'http://s.glbimg.com/es/ge/static/live/globoesporte/json/globoesporte-home-agregador.js',
                
                jsonpCallback: 'glbrealtime_callback',
                cache: true,
                success: function(json){
                    $.glbrealtime({
                        data: json,
                        debug: false
                    });
                }
            });
        });
    }

    var realtimeLoaded = false;

    $(window).on('load', function(){
        realtime(realtimeLoaded, "onLoad");
        realtimeLoaded = true;
    })

    setTimeout(function(){
        realtime(realtimeLoaded, "timeout")
        realtimeLoaded = true;
    }, 3000);
